Simple plain text exporter for demo purposes

See http://www.grantlee.org/apidox/for_themers.html for more information

Texture data:
    texture.width  = 7037
    texture.height = 1595

    texture.trimmedName = Disguise
    texture.fullName = Disguise.png
    texture.absoluteFileName = D:/InfiniteRunner/Assets/Textures/RahulSheets/Disguise.png

SmartUpdateHash: $TexturePacker:SmartUpdate:a4fbdd62d8e791ddf1fe17356fc3b560:54fd42763926eec2fc712fecc45ead15:c0a8a96fd9f031943ab7ac7ff06e471c$

Settings:

Access to all values in the settings (.tps file):

settings.tpsName                = unsaved ("unsaved" if used from command line without .tps file)
settings.allowRotation          = true
settings.autoAliasEnabled       = true
settings.flipPVR                = false
settings.forceIdenticalLayout   = false
settings.multiPack              = false
settings.premultiplyAlpha       = false
settings.shapeDebug             = false
settings.trimSpriteNames        = false
settings.fixedTextureSize       = -1 x -1
settings.dataFormat             = plain
settings.textureSubPath         = 
settings.ditherType             = NearestNeighbour
settings.outputFormat           = RGBA8888
settings.textureFormat          = png
settings.backgroundColor        = 0
settings.borderPadding          = 2
settings.shapePadding           = 2
settings.commonDivisorX         = 1
settings.commonDivisorY         = 1
settings.dpi                    = 72
settings.reduceBorderArtifacts  = false

settings.contentProtection.key  = 

Variants:

---
variant.scale = 1
variant.extension = 
variant.spriteFilter = 
variant.acceptFractionalValues = false
variant.maxTextureSize = -1 x -1



Not yet available:

settings.dataFileNames          = 
settings.textureFileName        = 
settings.algorithmSettings      = 
settings.globalSpriteSettings   = 

Adjusted values for the current autosd variant:

variantParams.scale             = 1
variantParams.shapePadding      = 2
variantParams.borderPadding     = 2
variantParams.commonDivisorX    = 1
variantParams.commonDivisorY    = 1
variantParams.extrude           = 0
variantParams.baseFactor        = 1
variantParams.maxTextureSize    = 8192 x 8192
variantParams.fixedTextureSize  = -1 x -1

Sprite data:

There are 2 variants:
- sprites - contains the sprites, aliases are available in the
  aliasList property and are not added top level

- allSprites - list of all sprites

Load javascript filter plugin, must be located in the exporter's folder in a subfolder
grantlee/0.2/makecssselector.qs


// set width & height for calculations using the javascript filter




    =========================================================================

    Use the javascript filter plugin to replace -hover with :hover
    Disguise31-Flip1.png

    -- name without image type extension
    sprite.trimmedName      = Disguise31-Flip1

    -- name with image extension
    sprite.fullName         = Disguise31-Flip1.png

    -- offset of the center of the trimmed sprite from the
    -- center of the original sprite (used by cocos2d)
    sprite.centerOffset.x = -35
    sprite.centerOffset.y = -113

    -- list of alias sprites for this one
    sprite.aliasList = 

    --- frame rectangle with pixel coordinates
    sprite.frameRect.x = 2
    sprite.frameRect.y = 2
    sprite.frameRect.width = 462
    sprite.frameRect.height = 674

    --- frame rectangle with uv coordinates (0..1)
    sprite.frameRectRel.x = 0.000284212022168538
    sprite.frameRectRel.y = 0.00125391849529781
    sprite.frameRectRel.width = 0.0656529771209322
    sprite.frameRectRel.height = 0.422570532915361

    --- frame rectangle with uv coordinates (0..1) calculated through JS
    sprite.frameRectRel.x = 0.0002842120221685377
    sprite.frameRectRel.y = 0.0002842120221685377
    sprite.frameRectRel.width = 0.06565297712093221
    sprite.frameRectRel.height = 0.09577945147079721

    --- version of the frame rect with "original" width and height
    sprite.frameRectWithoutRotation.x = 2
    sprite.frameRectWithoutRotation.y = 2
    sprite.frameRectWithoutRotation.width = 462
    sprite.frameRectWithoutRotation.height = 674

    -- true if the sprite was rotated
    sprite.rotated        = false

    -- true if the sprite does not contain any transparent pixels
    sprite.isSolid        = false

    -- true if the sprite was trimmed
    sprite.trimmed        = true

    sprite.sourceRect.x = 168
    sprite.sourceRect.y = 362
    sprite.sourceRect.width = 462
    sprite.sourceRect.height = 674

    sprite.cornerOffset.x = 168
    sprite.cornerOffset.y = 362

    sprite.untrimmedSize.width = 868
    sprite.untrimmedSize.height = 1172

    -- the file absolute file name of the sprite
    sprite.fileData.absoluteFileName = D:/InfiniteRunner/Assets/Textures/Disguise/Disguise31-Flip1.png

    -- the modification date of the sprite
    sprite.fileData.lastModified = 2015-01-27T19:54:06

    -- the creation date of the sprite
    sprite.fileData.created = 2015-01-28T00:03:31

    -- the file size of the sprite

### Values for the current texture
The following values are available inside templates that are written for each
variant or multipack. They are not available in a file that has the following values set:
<hasSeparateAutoSDFiles>all</hasSeparateAutoSDFiles>
<hasSeparateMultiPackFiles>last</hasSeparateMultiPackFiles>

## sprites
Contains the sprite of the current file, aliases are available through the aliasList property
Shortcut into texture.sprites

## allSprites
Contains all sprites of the current file including aliases.
Shortcut into texture.allSprites

## texture
Contains information about the current texture, size, and other information.
Shortcut into allResults[variantIndex].textures[multiPackIndex]

## variantParams
The data the current file was created with

### Values for all files
The following values are available for all templates

## settings
The main settigns the file was created with

## smartUpdateKey
The key for this file used to check file consistency and avoid re-calculating
data that is already available

## multiPackIndex
The multipack index number the current file was created with

## variantIndex
The AutoSD variant index the file was created with

## allResults
All texture and sprite information in a big array
